## Idea

Given a [cospan of types](foundation.cospans.md)

```text
  f : A → X ← B : g,
```

we can form the
{{#concept "standard pullback" Disambiguation="types" Agda=standard-pullback}}
`A ×_X B` satisfying
[the universal property of the pullback](foundation-core.universal-property-pullbacks.md)
of the cospan, completing the diagram

```text
  A ×_X B ------> B
     | ⌟          |
     |            | g
     |            |
     v            v
     A ---------> X.
           f
```

The standard pullback consists of [pairs](foundation.dependent-pair-types.md)
`a : A` and `b : B` such that `f a` and `g b` agree:

```text
  A ×_X B := Σ (a : A) (b : B), (f a ＝ g b).
```

Thus the standard [cone](foundation.cones-over-cospans.md) consists of the
canonical projections.

### The gap map into the standard pullback

The {{#concept "standard gap map" Disambiguation="cone over a cospan" Agda=gap}}
of a [commuting square](foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.md) is the map
from the domain of the cone into the standard pullback.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="3577" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="3584" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#3584" class="Module">_</a>

</pre>
### The small property of being a pullback

The [proposition](foundation-core.propositions.md) `is-pullback` is the
assertion that the gap map is an [equivalence](foundation-core.equivalences.md).
Note that this proposition is [small](foundation-core.small-types.md), whereas
[the universal property](foundation-core.universal-property-pullbacks.md) is a
large proposition.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4278" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4285" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4285" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="4289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4290" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4290" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="4293" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4293" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="4296" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4296" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="4299" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4299" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="4302" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4304" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4309" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4311" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4312" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4312" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4314" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4316" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4319" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4290" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="4321" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4323" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4324" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4324" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="4326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4328" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4331" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4293" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="4333" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4335" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4336" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4336" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4340" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4343" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4296" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="4345" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4347" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4348" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4348" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="4350" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4352" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4355" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#4299" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="4357" class="Symbol">}</a>

## Properties

### The standard pullback satisfies the universal property of pullbacks

    <a id="6640" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#6530" class="Function">universal-property-standard-pullback</a> <a id="6677" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#6677" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="6679" class="Symbol">=</a>

### The pullback of a Σ-type

Squares of the form

```text
  Σ (x : A) (Q (f x)) ----> Σ (y : B) Q
      |                          |
      |                          |
  pr1 |                          | pr1
      |                          |
      V                          V
      A -----------------------> B
                   f
```

are pullbacks.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="8887" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="8894" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8894" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="8898" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8899" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8899" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="8902" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8902" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="8905" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8905" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="8908" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8910" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="8915" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8917" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8918" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8918" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8920" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8922" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8925" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8899" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="8927" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8929" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8930" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8930" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8932" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8934" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8937" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8902" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="8939" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8941" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8942" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8942" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="8944" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8946" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8918" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8948" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8950" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8930" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8951" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8953" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8954" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8954" class="Bound">Q</a> <a id="8956" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8958" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8930" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8960" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8962" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="8965" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#8905" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="8967" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="8971" class="Keyword">where</a>

      <a id="10783" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10785" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#9990" class="Function">is-pullback-cone-standard-pullback-Σ</a><a id="10821" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Pullbacks are symmetric

The pullback of `f : A → X ← B : g` is also the pullback of `g : B → X ← A : f`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="map-commutative-standard-pullback"></a><a id="10947" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10947" class="Function">map-commutative-standard-pullback</a> <a id="10981" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="10985" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10986" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10986" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="10989" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10989" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="10992" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10992" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="10995" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10997" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="11002" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11004" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11005" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11005" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11007" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11009" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="11012" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10986" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="11014" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11016" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11017" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11017" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="11019" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11021" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="11024" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10989" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="11026" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11028" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11029" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11029" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="11031" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11033" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="11036" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10992" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="11038" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="11042" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11043" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11043" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11045" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11047" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11005" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11049" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11051" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11029" class="Bound">X</a><a id="11052" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11054" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11055" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11055" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11057" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11059" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11017" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="11061" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11063" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11029" class="Bound">X</a><a id="11064" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11066" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11068" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2266" class="Function">standard-pullback</a> <a id="11086" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11043" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11088" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11055" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11090" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11092" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2266" class="Function">standard-pullback</a> <a id="11110" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11055" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11112" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11043" class="Bound">f</a>
<a id="11114" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#603" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="11118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11119" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10947" class="Function">map-commutative-standard-pullback</a> <a id="11153" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11153" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11155" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11155" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11157" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11157" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11158" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11160" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="11164" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2563" class="Function">horizontal-map-standard-pullback</a> <a id="11197" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11157" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="11199" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#603" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="11203" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11204" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="11208" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11209" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10947" class="Function">map-commutative-standard-pullback</a> <a id="11243" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11243" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11245" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11245" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11247" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11247" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11248" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11251" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="11255" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#2462" class="Function">vertical-map-standard-pullback</a> <a id="11286" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11247" class="Bound">x</a>
<a id="11288" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="11292" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11293" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types.html#615" class="Field">pr2</a> <a id="11297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11298" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#10947" class="Function">map-commutative-standard-pullback</a> <a id="11332" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11332" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="11334" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11334" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="11336" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11336" class="Bound">x</a><a id="11337" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="11340" class="Symbol">=</a>

      <a id="13791" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13793" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#11766" class="Function">is-equiv-map-commutative-standard-pullback</a> <a id="13836" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#13588" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13838" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#13590" class="Bound">g</a><a id="13839" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Pullbacks can be "folded"

Given a pullback square

```text
         f'
    C -------> B
    | ⌟        |
  g'|          | g
    v          v
    A -------> X
         f
```

we can "fold" the vertical edge onto the horizontal one and get a new pullback
square

```text
            C ---------> X
            | ⌟          |
  (f' , g') |            |
            v            v
          A × B -----> X × X,
                f × g
```

moreover, this folded square is a pullback if and only if the original one is.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="14373" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14380" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14380" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="14384" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14385" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14385" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="14388" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14388" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="14391" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14391" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="14394" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14396" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="14401" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14405" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14406" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14406" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14410" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="14413" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14385" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="14415" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14417" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14418" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14418" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14420" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14422" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="14425" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14388" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="14427" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14429" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14430" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14430" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="14432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14434" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="14437" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14391" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="14439" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="14443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14444" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14444" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14448" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14406" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14452" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14430" class="Bound">X</a><a id="14453" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14455" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14456" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14456" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14460" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14418" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14464" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#14430" class="Bound">X</a><a id="14465" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="22092" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22094" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#18436" class="Function">map-prod-cone</a> <a id="22108" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#19562" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="22110" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#19574" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="22112" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#19586" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="22115" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#19601" class="Bound">g&#39;</a><a id="22117" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="22178" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22180" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#20030" class="Function">triangle-map-prod-cone</a> <a id="22203" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#21847" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="22205" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#21849" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="22207" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="22265" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="22267" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#21852" class="Bound">is-pb-cc&#39;</a><a id="22276" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### A family of maps over a base map induces a pullback square if and only if it is a family of equivalences

Given a map `f : A → B` with a family of maps over it
`g : (x : A) → P x → Q (f x)`, then the square

```text
         map-Σ f g
  Σ A P ----------> Σ B Q
    |                |
    |                |
    v                v
    A -------------> B
             f
```

is a pullback if and only if `g` is a
[fiberwise equivalence](foundation-core.families-of-equivalences.md).

<pre class="Agda"><a id="22778" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="22785" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#22785" class="Module">_</a>

### A cone is a pullback if and only if it induces a family of equivalences between the fibers of the vertical maps

### The horizontal pullback pasting property

Given a diagram as follows where the right-hand square is a pullback

```text
  ∙ -------> ∙ -------> ∙
  |          | ⌟        |
  |          |          |
  v          v          v
  ∙ -------> ∙ -------> ∙,
```

then the left-hand square is a pullback if and only if the composite square is.

              <a id="29717" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29719" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#28758" class="Bound">is-pb-rect</a><a id="29729" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="29745" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29747" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#28898" class="Bound">x</a><a id="29748" class="Symbol">)))</a>
</pre>
### The vertical pullback pasting property

Given a diagram as follows where the lower square is a pullback

```text
  ∙ -------> ∙
  |          |
  |          |
  v          v
  ∙ -------> ∙
  | ⌟        |
  |          |
  v          v
  ∙ -------> ∙,
```

then the upper square is a pullback if and only if the composite square is.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="30100" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="30107" href="foundation-core.pullbacks.html#30107" class="Module">_</a>
